namespace = pw_wonder

# Initial event to say this mod is active.
country_event = {
	id = pw_wonder.0
	hide_window = yes
	# is_triggered_only = yes
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 1 }
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_global_flag = pw_active }
	}
	immediate = { set_global_flag = pw_active }
}

#Message for wonder construction complete
# UNUSED!
planet_event = {
	id = pw_wonder.1
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	pre_triggers = {
		has_owner = yes
		is_occupied_flag = no
	}

	immediate = {
		create_message = {
			type = PW_WONDER_COMPLETED
			localization = pw_message_space_elevator_complete
			days = 30
			target = this
			variable = {
				type = name
				localization = WONDER
				scope = from
			}
			variable = {
				type = name
				localization = PLANET
				scope = root
			}
		}
	}
}

#Added by Celestial Monuments Tradition: Gain Unity when Megastructure upgraded
#Triggered when megastructure is build(?) or upgraded
country_event = {
	id = pw_wonder.10
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_tradition = tr_pw_monumentality_celestial_monuments
		from = {
			NOT = { has_megastructure_flag = pw_megastructure_gave_unity_recently }
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		from = {
			set_timed_megastructure_flag = {
				flag = pw_megastructure_gave_unity_recently
				days = 360
			}
		}
		add_monthly_resource_mult = {
			resource = unity
			value = @tier3unityreward
			min = 500
			max = @tier3unitymax
		}
	}
}

# Space Elevator -> id 100

#On Space Elevator built
planet_event = {
	id = pw_wonder.100
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	pre_triggers = {
		has_owner = yes
	}

	immediate = {
		create_message = {
			type = PW_WONDER_COMPLETED
			localization = pw_message_space_elevator_complete
			days = 30
			target = this
			variable = {
				type = name
				localization = PLANET
				scope = root
			}
		}

		planet_event = { id = pw_wonder.101 }
		planet_event = { id = pw_wonder.102 }
		planet_event = { id = pw_wonder.103 days = 5 }
	}
}

#On first time Space Elevator is built (regular empire)
planet_event = {
	id = pw_wonder.101
	title = pw_wonder.101.name
	desc = pw_wonder.101.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_pw_space_elevator
	show_sound = event_construction
	is_triggered_only = yes
	location = this

	trigger = {
		NOT = {owner = {has_country_flag = pw_space_elevator_built }}
		owner = { is_gestalt = no }
	}

	immediate = {
		owner = { set_country_flag = pw_space_elevator_built }
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.101.a
		add_modifier = {
			modifier = pw_mod_space_elevator_xenophile
			days = @pw_5years
			clear_on_owner_change = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.101.b
		add_modifier = {
			modifier = pw_mod_space_elevator_xenophobe
			days = @pw_5years
			clear_on_owner_change = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.101.c

		trigger = {
			owner = {
				is_eager_explorer_empire = yes
			}
		}

		add_modifier = {
			modifier = pw_mod_space_elevator_explorers
			days = @pw_5years
			clear_on_owner_change = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.101.d

		trigger = {
			owner = {
				OR = {
					has_valid_civic = civic_ascensionists
					has_valid_civic = civic_corporate_ascensionists
				}
			}
		}

		add_modifier = {
			modifier = pw_mod_space_elevator_ladder_to_the_sky
			days = @pw_5years
			clear_on_owner_change = yes
		}
	}

	after = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOR = {
					has_modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_happiness
					has_modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_unity
				}
			}
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_happiness
				days = @pw_5years
			}
		}
	}
}

#On first time Space Elevator is built (gestalt)
planet_event = {
	id = pw_wonder.102
	title = pw_wonder.102.name
	desc = pw_wonder.102.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_pw_space_elevator
	show_sound = event_construction
	is_triggered_only = yes
	location = this

	trigger = {
		NOT = {owner = {has_country_flag = pw_space_elevator_built }}
		owner = { is_gestalt = yes }
	}

	immediate = {
		owner = { set_country_flag = pw_space_elevator_built }
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.102.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOR = {
					has_modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_happiness
					has_modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_unity
				}
			}
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_unity
				days = @pw_5years
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.102.b
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOR = {
					has_modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_happiness
					has_modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_unity
				}
			}
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_unity
				days = @pw_5years
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.102.c

		trigger = {
			owner = {
				is_eager_explorer_empire = yes
			}
		}
		owner = {
			add_monthly_resource_mult = {
				resource = unity
				value = @tier2unityreward
				min = @tier2unitymin
				max = @tier2unitymax
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.102.d

		trigger = {
			owner = {
				OR = {
					has_valid_civic = civic_hive_ascensionists
					has_valid_civic = civic_machine_ascensionists
				}
			}
		}

		add_modifier = {
			modifier = pw_mod_space_elevator_ladder_to_the_sky
			days = @pw_5years
			clear_on_owner_change = yes
		}
	}

	after = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOR = {
					has_modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_happiness
					has_modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_unity
				}
			}
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_unity
				days = @pw_5years
			}
		}
	}
}

#Random choice of event after Space Elevator is build.
planet_event = {
	id = pw_wonder.103
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_active_building = pw_building_space_elevator
	}

	immediate = {
		random_list = {
			10 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					owner = { is_gestalt = yes }
				}
				planet_event = { id = pw_wonder.104 days = 180 random = 180 }
			}
			10 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					owner = { is_gestalt = yes }
				}
				planet_event = { id = pw_wonder.105 days = 180 random = 180 }
			}
			10 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					owner = { is_gestalt = yes }
				}
				planet_event = { id = pw_wonder.106 days = 180 random = 180 }
			}
			10 = {
				planet_event = { id = pw_wonder.107 days = 180 random = 180 }
			}
		}
	}
}

#Seize unregulated goods
planet_event = {
	id = pw_wonder.104
	title = pw_wonder.104.name
	desc = pw_wonder.104.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_pw_space_elevator
	show_sound = event_cityscape
	is_triggered_only = yes
	location = this

	trigger = {
		NOT = { owner = { has_country_flag = pw_wonder_event_104 }}
		has_active_building = pw_building_space_elevator
	}
	immediate = {
		owner = { set_timed_country_flag = { flag = pw_wonder_event_104 days = @pw_5years }}
	}
	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.104.a
		owner = {
			add_monthly_resource_mult = {
				resource = consumer_goods
				value = @tier3materialreward
				min = @tier3materialmin
				max = @tier3materialmax
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.104.b
		owner = {
			add_monthly_resource_mult = {
				resource = energy
				value = @tier3materialreward
				min = @tier3materialmin
				max = @tier3materialmax
			}
		}
	}
}

#Stowaways
planet_event = {
	id = pw_wonder.106
	title = pw_wonder.106.name
	desc = pw_wonder.106.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_pw_space_elevator
	show_sound = event_cityscape
	is_triggered_only = yes
	location = this

	trigger = {
		NOT = { owner = { has_country_flag = pw_wonder_event_106 }}
		has_active_building = pw_building_space_elevator
	}
	immediate = {
		owner = { set_timed_country_flag = { flag = pw_wonder_event_106 days = @pw_5years }}
	}
	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.106.a
		create_pop = {
			species = owner
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.106.b
		custom_tooltip = pw_wonder.106.b.tooltip
		owner = {
			create_fleet = {
				name = "Stowaways"
				effect = {
					set_owner = root.owner
					set_location = root
					create_ship = {
						name = random
						design = "NAME_Colonizer"
						colonizer_species = root.owner.owner_species
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.106.c
		owner = {
			owner = {
				add_monthly_resource_mult = {
					resource = influence
					value = @tier2influencereward
					min = @tier2influencemin
					max = @tier2influencemax
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Kessler Effect -> Convert to situation!
planet_event = {
	id = pw_wonder.107
	title = pw_wonder.107.name
	desc = pw_wonder.107.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_pw_space_elevator
	show_sound = event_cityscape
	is_triggered_only = yes
	location = this

	trigger = {
		NOT = { owner = { has_country_flag = pw_wonder_event_107 }}
		has_active_building = pw_building_space_elevator
	}
	immediate = {
		owner = { set_timed_country_flag = { flag = pw_wonder_event_107 days = @pw_5years }}
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.107.a
		allow = {
			owner = {
				resource_stockpile_compare = {
					resource = energy
					value >= 2000
				}
			}
		}
		owner = {
			add_resource = {
				energy = -2000
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.107.b
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = { is_gestalt = yes }
			}
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = pw_mod_space_elevator_kessler_effect_no_happiness
				days = @pw_5years
			}
		}
		else ={
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = pw_mod_space_elevator_kessler_effect
				days = @pw_5years
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.107.c
		trigger = {
			owner = { is_gestalt = no }
		}
		allow = {
			owner = {
				resource_stockpile_compare = {
					resource = influence
					value >= 25
				}
			}
		}
		owner = {
			add_resource = {
				influence = -25
			}
		}
		add_modifier = {
			modifier = pw_mod_space_elevator_kessler_effect
			days = @pw_2years
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.107.d
		trigger = {
			owner = { is_scavenger = yes }
		}
		allow = {
			owner = {
				resource_stockpile_compare = {
					resource = energy
					value >= 3000
				}
			}
		}
		owner = {
			add_resource = {
				energy = -3000
				alloys = 500
			}
		}
	}
}

#Help Development
planet_event = {
	id = pw_wonder.110
	title = pw_wonder.110.name
	desc = pw_wonder.110.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_pw_space_elevator
	show_sound = event_cityscape
	is_triggered_only = yes
	location = this

	trigger = {
		solar_system = {
			NOT = { has_star_flag = pw_wonder_event_110 }
			any_system_planet = {
				has_active_building = pw_building_space_elevator
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		solar_system = {
			set_timed_star_flag = { flag = pw_wonder_event_110 days = @pw_5years }
			random_system_planet = {
				limit = { has_active_building = pw_building_space_elevator }
				save_event_target_as = pw_space_elevator_aid_dev_planet
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.110.a
		allow = {
			owner = {
				resource_stockpile_compare = {
					resource = energy
					value >= 500
				}
				resource_stockpile_compare = {
					resource = minerals
					value >= 500
				}
			}
		}
		owner = {
			add_resource = {
				energy = -500
				minerals = -500
			}
		}
		add_modifier = {
			modifier = pw_mod_space_elevator_aided_development_colonization
			clear_on_owner_change = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.110.b
	}
}

#Help Development (Finish Colonization)
planet_event = {
	id = pw_wonder.111
	title = pw_wonder.111.name
	desc = pw_wonder.111.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_pw_space_elevator
	show_sound = event_cityscape
	is_triggered_only = yes
	location = this

	trigger = {
		has_modifier = pw_mod_space_elevator_aided_development_colonization
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.111.a
		if = {
			limit = { has_modifier = pw_mod_space_elevator_aided_development_colonization }
			remove_modifier = pw_mod_space_elevator_aided_development_colonization
		}
		add_modifier = {
			modifier = pw_mod_space_elevator_aided_development_established
			days = @pw_5years
			clear_on_owner_change = yes
		}
	}
}

#On both Skyhook and Space Ramp have been constructed
planet_event = {
	id = pw_wonder.120
	title = pw_wonder.120.name
	desc = pw_wonder.120.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_pw_space_elevator
	show_sound = event_cityscape
	is_triggered_only = yes
	location = this

	trigger = {
		has_active_building = pw_building_space_elevator
		has_deposit = pw_d_SE_skyhook
		OR = {
			has_deposit = pw_d_SE_space_ramp
			has_deposit = pw_d_SE_nuclear_launcher
		}
		owner = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = pw_wonder_event_120 }
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		owner = {
			set_country_flag = pw_wonder_event_120
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.120.a
		owner = {
			add_monthly_resource_mult = {
				resource = influence
				value = @tier2influencereward
				min = @tier2influencemin
				max = @tier2influencemax
			}
		}
	}
}

#On counterweigh habitat is colonized
planet_event = {
	id = pw_wonder.121
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	location = this

	trigger = {
		merg_is_habitat = yes
		exists = orbit
		orbit = {
			has_active_building = pw_building_space_elevator
		}
		exists = owner
		owner = {
			has_technology = pw_tech_space_elevator_counterweight_habitat
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_modifier = pw_mod_space_elevator_counterweight_habitat }}
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = pw_mod_space_elevator_counterweight_habitat
			}
		}
	}
}

#Open for Galactic Market decision
planet_event = {
	id = pw_wonder.130
	title = pw_wonder.130.name
	desc = pw_wonder.130.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_pw_space_elevator
	is_triggered_only = yes
	location = this

	immediate = {
		set_planet_flag = pw_SE_is_choosing_market_bonus
	}

	trigger = {
		has_active_building = pw_building_space_elevator
		NOT = { has_planet_flag = pw_SE_is_choosing_market_bonus }
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.130.a
		custom_tooltip = pw_wonder.130.tooltip
		pw_remove_galactic_market_modifiers = yes
		if = {
			limit = { owner = { is_gestalt = no }}
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = pw_mod_space_elevator_open_market_free_assets_concession
				clear_on_owner_change = yes
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = pw_mod_space_elevator_open_market_free_assets_concession_gestalt
				clear_on_owner_change = yes
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.130.b
		custom_tooltip = pw_wonder.130.tooltip
		trigger = {
			owner = { is_galactic_community_member = yes }
		}
		allow = {
			owner = {
				OR = {
					is_active_resolution = resolution_industry_building_a_better_tomorrow
					is_active_resolution = resolution_industry_environmental_ordinance_waivers
					is_active_resolution = resolution_industry_project_cornucopia
				}
			}
		}
		pw_remove_galactic_market_modifiers = yes
		if = {
			limit = { owner = { is_gestalt = no }}
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = pw_mod_space_elevator_open_market_industrial_protectionism
				clear_on_owner_change = yes
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = pw_mod_space_elevator_open_market_industrial_protectionism_gestalt
				clear_on_owner_change = yes
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.130.c
		custom_tooltip = pw_wonder.130.tooltip
		trigger = {
			owner = { is_galactic_community_member = yes }
		}
		allow = {
			owner = {
				OR = {
					is_active_resolution = resolution_greatergood_greater_than_ourselves
					is_active_resolution = resolution_greatergood_balance_in_the_middle
					is_active_resolution = resolution_greatergood_universal_prosperity_mandate
				}
			}
		}
		pw_remove_galactic_market_modifiers = yes
		if = {
			limit = { owner = { is_gestalt = no }}
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = pw_mod_space_elevator_open_market_intergalactic_unions
				clear_on_owner_change = yes
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = pw_mod_space_elevator_open_market_intergalactic_unions_gestalt
				clear_on_owner_change = yes
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.130.d
		custom_tooltip = pw_wonder.130.tooltip
		trigger = {
			owner = { is_galactic_community_member = yes }
		}
		allow = {
			owner = {
				OR = {
					is_active_resolution = resolution_ecology_integrated_gardens
					is_active_resolution = resolution_ecology_environmental_control_board
					is_active_resolution = resolution_ecology_paradise_initiative
				}
			}
		}
		pw_remove_galactic_market_modifiers = yes
		if = {
			limit = { owner = { is_gestalt = no }}
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = pw_mod_space_elevator_open_market_local_extraction_subsides
				clear_on_owner_change = yes
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = pw_mod_space_elevator_open_market_local_extraction_subsides_gestalt
				clear_on_owner_change = yes
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.130.e
		custom_tooltip = pw_wonder.130.tooltip
		trigger = {
			owner = { is_galactic_community_member = yes }
		}
		allow = {
			owner = {
				OR = {
					is_active_resolution = resolution_galacticstudies_advanced_xenostudies
					is_active_resolution = resolution_galacticstudies_ethical_guideline_refactoring
					is_active_resolution = resolution_galacticstudies_extradimensional_experimentation
				}
			}
		}
		pw_remove_galactic_market_modifiers = yes
		if = {
			limit = { owner = { is_gestalt = no }}
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = pw_mod_space_elevator_open_market_local_content_requirements
				clear_on_owner_change = yes
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = pw_mod_space_elevator_open_market_local_content_requirements_gestalt
				clear_on_owner_change = yes
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_planet_flag = pw_SE_is_choosing_market_bonus
		}
	}
}

# Particle Supercollider -> id 200

#On Particle Supercollider built
planet_event = {
	id = pw_wonder.200
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	pre_triggers = {
		has_owner = yes
	}

	immediate = {
		create_message = {
			type = PW_WONDER_COMPLETED
			localization = pw_message_particle_supercollider_complete
			days = 30
			target = this
			variable = {
				type = name
				localization = PLANET
				scope = root
			}
		}

		planet_event = { id = pw_wonder.201 }
		planet_event = { id = pw_wonder.202 }
		owner = { country_event = { #Subject/Overlord events
			id = pw_wonder.203
			days = 10
		}}
	}
}

#On first time Particle Supercollider is built (Regular Empire)
planet_event = {
	id = pw_wonder.201
	title = pw_wonder.201.name
	desc = pw_wonder.201.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_physics_research
	show_sound = event_construction
	is_triggered_only = yes
	location = this

	trigger = {
		NOT = {owner = {has_country_flag = pw_particle_supercollider_built }}
		owner = { is_gestalt = no }
	}

	immediate = {
		owner = { set_country_flag = pw_particle_supercollider_built }
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.201.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOR = {
					has_modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_happiness
					has_modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_unity
				}
			}
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_happiness
				days = @pw_5years
			}
		}
		add_modifier = {
			modifier = pw_mod_particle_supercollider_materialist
			days = @pw_5years
			clear_on_owner_change = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.201.b
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOR = {
					has_modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_happiness
					has_modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_unity
				}
			}
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_happiness
				days = @pw_5years
			}
		}
		add_modifier = {
			modifier = pw_mod_particle_supercollider_spiritualist
			days = @pw_5years
			clear_on_owner_change = yes
		}
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			owner = {
				country_event = { #Fallen Empire Event
					id = pw_research.999
					days = 30
					random = 30
				}
				country_event = { #Experiments
					id = pw_research.1100
					days = @pw_1year
					random = 30
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Rewards a bulwark for building GA
country_event = {
	id = pw_wonder.203
	title = pw_wonder.203.name
	desc = pw_wonder.203.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_physics_research
	show_sound = event_laboratory_sound
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		exists = overlord
		is_specialist_subject_type = { TYPE = scholarium }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = pw_particle_supercollider_scholarium_subject }
	}

	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = pw_particle_supercollider_scholarium_subject
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.203.a
		add_monthly_resource_mult = {
			resource = unity
			value = @tier1unityreward
			min = @tier1unitymin
			max = @tier1unitymax
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.203.b
		add_monthly_resource_mult = {
			resource = unity
			value = @tier1unityreward
			min = @tier1unitymin
			max = @tier1unitymax
		}
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			overlord = {
				country_event = { id = pw_wonder.204 }
			}
		}
	}
}

#Notifies overlord when a Bulwark builds GA

	id = pw_wonder.250
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

		has_owner = yes
	}

	trigger = {
		#This would be triggered every time a building is upgraded.

	}

	immediate = {
		create_message = {
			type = PW_WONDER_COMPLETED

			variable = {
				type = name
				localization = PLANET
				scope = root
			}
		}

		planet_event = { id = pw_wonder.251 } #first time
	}
}

# Domed City -> id 300

#On Domed City built
planet_event = {
	id = pw_wonder.300
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	pre_triggers = {
		has_owner = yes
	}

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { merg_is_habitat = yes }
			create_message = {
				type = PW_WONDER_COMPLETED
				localization = pw_message_secluded_sector_complete
				days = 30
				target = this
				variable = {
					type = name
					localization = PLANET
					scope = root
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			create_message = {
				type = PW_WONDER_COMPLETED
				localization = pw_message_domed_city_complete
				days = 30
				target = this
				variable = {
					type = name
					localization = PLANET
					scope = root
				}
			}
		}

		planet_event = { id = pw_wonder.301 }
		planet_event = { id = pw_wonder.302 }
	}
}

#On first time Domed City is built (Regular Empire)
planet_event = {
	id = pw_wonder.301
	title = pw_wonder.301.name
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = { merg_is_habitat = yes }
		}
		text = pw_wonder.301.desc.planet
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			merg_is_habitat = yes
		}
		text = pw_wonder.301.desc.habitat
	}

	picture = GFX_evt_pw_domed_city
	show_sound = event_construction
	is_triggered_only = yes
	location = this

	trigger = {
		NOT = {owner = {has_country_flag = pw_domed_city_built }}
		owner = { is_gestalt = no }
	}

	immediate = {
		owner = { set_country_flag = pw_domed_city_built }
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.301.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOR = {
					has_modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_happiness
					has_modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_unity
				}
			}
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_happiness
				days = @pw_5years
			}
		}
		add_modifier = {
			modifier = pw_mod_domed_city_egalitarian
			days = @pw_5years
			clear_on_owner_change = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.301.b
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOR = {
					has_modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_happiness
					has_modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_unity
				}
			}
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_happiness
				days = @pw_5years
			}
		}
		add_modifier = {
			modifier = pw_mod_domed_city_authoritarian
			days = @pw_5years
			clear_on_owner_change = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.301.c
		trigger = {
			owner = {
				is_overlord = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOR = {
					has_modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_happiness
					has_modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_unity
				}
			}
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_happiness
				days = @pw_5years
			}
		}
		add_modifier = {
			modifier = pw_mod_domed_city_authoritarian
			days = @pw_5years
			clear_on_owner_change = yes
		}
		owner = {
			add_monthly_resource_mult = {
				resource = unity
				value = @tier1unityreward
				min = @tier1unitymin
				max = @tier1unitymax
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			owner = {
				country_event = { #Fallen Empire Event
					id = pw_research.1999
					days = 30
					random = 30
				}
				country_event = { #Hyper-Reality Show
					id = pw_research.2010
					days = 300
				}
				country_event = { #Experiments
					id = pw_research.2100
					days = @pw_1year
					random = 30
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = pw_wonder.351
	title = pw_wonder.351.name
	desc = pw_wonder.351.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_pw_domed_city
	show_sound = event_construction
	is_triggered_only = yes
	location = this

	pre_triggers = {
		has_owner = yes
	}

		NOT = {owner = { has_country_flag = pw_psionic_observatory_built }}
	}

	immediate = {
		owner = { set_country_flag = pw_psionic_observatory_built }
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.351.a
		trigger = {
			exists = owner
			owner = {
				OR = {
					is_spiritualist = yes
					has_ascension_perk = ap_mind_over_matter
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_modifier = pw_mod_research_inspiration }
			}
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = pw_mod_research_inspiration
				days = @pw_5years
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.351.b
		trigger = {
			exists = owner
			owner = { NOT = { has_ascension_perk = ap_mind_over_matter }}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_modifier = pw_mod_research_inspiration }
			}
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = pw_mod_research_inspiration
				days = @pw_5years
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		planet_event = {
			id = pw_wonder.355
			days = 10
		}
	}
}

		}
		add_modifier = {
			modifier = pw_mod_abyssal_test_crater_militarist
			days = @pw_5years
			clear_on_owner_change = yes
		}
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			owner = {
				country_event = { #Fallen Empire Event
					id = pw_research.2999
					days = 30
					random = 30
				}
				country_event = { #Experiments
					id = pw_research.3100
					days = @pw_1year
					random = 30
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#On first time Abyssal Crater Test Site is built (Gestalt)

# Metal Vivarium -> id 450

#On Metal Vivarium built
planet_event = {
	id = pw_wonder.450
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	pre_triggers = {
		has_owner = yes
	}

	trigger = {
		#This would be triggered every time a building is upgraded.
		last_building_changed = pw_building_metal_vivarium
	}

	immediate = {
		create_message = {
			type = PW_WONDER_COMPLETED
			localization = pw_message_metal_vivarium_complete
			days = 30
			target = this
			variable = {
				type = name
				localization = PLANET
				scope = root
			}
		}

		planet_event = { id = pw_wonder.451 } #first time
	}
}

#On first time Metal Vivarium is built
planet_event = {
	id = pw_wonder.451
	title = pw_wonder.451.name
	desc = pw_wonder.451.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_pw_abyssal_crater_test_site
	show_sound = event_construction
	is_triggered_only = yes
	location = this

	pre_triggers = {
		has_owner = yes
	}

	trigger = {
		NOT = {owner = { has_country_flag = pw_metal_vivarium_built }}
	}

	immediate = {
		owner = { set_country_flag = pw_metal_vivarium_built }
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.451.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_modifier = pw_mod_research_inspiration }
			}
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = pw_mod_research_inspiration
				days = @pw_5years
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		planet_event = {
			id = pw_wonder.455
			days = 10
		}
	}
}

# Erebus Project -> id 500

#On Erebus Project built
planet_event = {
	id = pw_wonder.500
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	pre_triggers = {
		has_owner = yes
	}

	immediate = {
		create_message = {
			type = PW_WONDER_COMPLETED
			localization = pw_message_erebus_project_complete
			days = 30
			target = this
			variable = {
				type = name
				localization = PLANET
				scope = root
			}
		}

		planet_event = { id = pw_wonder.501 }
		planet_event = { id = pw_wonder.502 }
	}
}

#On first time Erebus Project is built (Regular Empire)
planet_event = {
	id = pw_wonder.501
	title = pw_wonder.501.name
	desc = pw_wonder.501.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_pw_erebus_project
	show_sound = event_construction
	is_triggered_only = yes
	location = this

	trigger = {
		NOT = {owner = { has_country_flag = pw_erebus_project_built }}
		owner = { is_gestalt = no }
	}

	immediate = {
		owner = { set_country_flag = pw_erebus_project_built }
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.501.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOR = {
					has_modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_happiness
					has_modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_unity
				}
			}
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_happiness
				days = @pw_5years
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.501.b
		trigger = {
			owner = {
				has_valid_civic = civic_mining_guilds
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOR = {
					has_modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_happiness
					has_modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_unity
				}
			}
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_happiness
				days = @pw_5years
			}
		}
		owner = {
			add_monthly_resource_mult = {
				resource = unity
				value = @tier2unityreward
				min = @tier2unitymin
				max = @tier2unitymax
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.501.c
		trigger = {
			owner = {
				is_lithoid = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOR = {
					has_modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_happiness
					has_modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_unity
				}
			}
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_happiness
				days = @pw_5years
				multiplier = 2
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.501.d
		trigger = {
			owner = {
				has_origin = origin_subterranean
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOR = {
					has_modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_happiness
					has_modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_unity
				}
			}
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_happiness
				days = @pw_5years
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					has_origin = origin_subterranean
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = pw_wonder.501.tooltip
		}
	}
}

#On first time Erebus Project is built (Gestalt)
planet_event = {
	id = pw_wonder.502
	title = pw_wonder.502.name
	desc = pw_wonder.502.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_pw_erebus_project
	show_sound = event_construction
	is_triggered_only = yes
	location = this

	trigger = {
		NOT = {owner = { has_country_flag = pw_erebus_project_built }}
		owner = { is_gestalt = yes }
	}

	immediate = {
		owner = { set_country_flag = pw_erebus_project_built }
	}

				NOR = {
					has_modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_happiness

				}
			}
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_unity
				days = @pw_5years
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.502.b
		trigger = {
			owner = {
				has_valid_civic = civic_machine_rockbreakers
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOR = {
					has_modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_happiness
					has_modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_unity
				}

		}

	option = {

			owner = {
				is_lithoid = yes
				NOT = { has_civic = civic_hive_devouring_swarm }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOR = {

		}
		if = {

				NOR = {
					has_modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_happiness
					has_modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_unity
				}
			}
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_unity
				days = @pw_5years
				multiplier = 2
			}
		}
		owner = {
			add_monthly_resource_mult = {
				resource = unity
				value = @tier2unityreward
				min = @tier2unitymin
				max = @tier2unitymax
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.501.d
		trigger = {
			owner = {
				has_origin = origin_subterranean
			}
		}
		if = {

					has_modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_happiness
					has_modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_unity

		}
	}
}

#Random Aggressive Prospecting effect
planet_event = {
	id = pw_wonder.503
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_planet_flag = pw_aggressive_prospecting_event_triggered }
		has_modifier = pw_mod_erebus_prospecting
	}

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { #Exhausted mining options.
				has_planet_flag = pw_aggressive_prospecting_crystal
				has_planet_flag = pw_aggressive_prospecting_motes
				has_planet_flag = pw_aggressive_prospecting_gases
			}
			planet_event = {
				id = pw_wonder.510
				days = 60
				random = 30
			}
		}
		else = {
			random_list = {
				10 = {
					planet_event = {
						id = pw_wonder.504
						days = 60
						random = 30
					}
				}
				10 = {
					planet_event = {
						id = pw_wonder.506
						days = 60
						random = 30
					}
				}
				10 = {
					planet_event = {
						id = pw_wonder.508
						days = 60
						random = 30
					}
				}
				10 = {}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Check if already added crystals
planet_event = {
	id = pw_wonder.504
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	location = this

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_active_building = pw_building_erebus_project
			has_active_building = pw_building_erebus_fracking_plant
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_planet_flag = pw_aggressive_prospecting_crystal }
			planet_event = { id = pw_wonder.503 }
		}
		else = {
			planet_event = { id = pw_wonder.505 }
		}
	}
}

			add_modifier = {
				modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_happiness
				days = @pw_5years
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.601.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				owner = { is_megacorp = yes }
				owner = { has_valid_civic = civic_corporate_dominion }
				owner = { has_valid_civic = civic_merchant_guilds }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOR = {
					has_modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_happiness
					has_modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_unity
				}
			}
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_happiness
				days = @pw_10years
			}
		}
	}
}

#Random Cloud Seeding effect
planet_event = {
	id = pw_wonder.603
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_planet_flag = pw_cloud_seeding_event_triggered }
	}

	immediate = {
		set_planet_flag = pw_cloud_seeding_event_triggered
		random_list = {
			10 = {
				planet_event = {
					id = pw_wonder.604
					days = 60
					random = 30
				}
			}
			10 = {
				planet_event = {
					id = pw_wonder.605
					days = 60
					random = 30
				}
			}
			10 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					OR = {
						merg_is_machine_world = yes
						merg_is_hive_world = yes
					}
				}
				planet_event = {
					id = pw_wonder.606
					days = 60
					random = 30
				}
			}
			5 = {}
		}
	}
}

#Cloud Seeding adds Hazardous Weather
planet_event = {
	id = pw_wonder.604
	title = pw_wonder.604.name
	desc = pw_wonder.604.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_pw_helios_tower
	show_sound = event_cityscape
	is_triggered_only = yes
	location = this

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_modifier = hazardous_weather }
		OR = {
			has_active_building = pw_building_helios_tower
			has_active_building = pw_building_helios_translucent_obelisk
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.604.a
		add_modifier = {
			modifier = hazardous_weather
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.604.b
		allow = {
			owner = {
				resource_stockpile_compare = {
					resource = energy
					value >= 1000
				}
			}
		}
		owner = {
			add_resource = {
				energy = -1000
			}
		}
	}
}

# Helios Translucent Obelisk -> id 600

#On Helios Translucent Obelisk built
planet_event = {
	id = pw_wonder.650
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	pre_triggers = {
		has_owner = yes
	}

	trigger = {
		#This would be triggered every time a building is upgraded.
		last_building_changed = pw_building_helios_translucent_obelisk
	}

	immediate = {
		create_message = {
			type = PW_WONDER_COMPLETED
			localization = pw_message_helios_translucent_obelisk_complete
			days = 30
			target = this
			variable = {
				type = name
				localization = PLANET
				scope = root
			}
		}

		planet_event = { id = pw_wonder.651 }
	}
}

#On first time Helios Translucent Obelisk is built (Regular Empire)
planet_event = {
	id = pw_wonder.651
	title = pw_wonder.651.name
	desc = pw_wonder.651.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_pw_helios_tower
	show_sound = event_construction
	is_triggered_only = yes
	location = this

	trigger = {
		NOT = {owner = { has_country_flag = pw_helios_translucent_obelisk_built }}
	}

	immediate = {
		owner = { set_country_flag = pw_helios_translucent_obelisk_built }
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.651.a
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.651.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				owner = { is_megacorp = yes }
				owner = { has_valid_civic = civic_corporate_dominion }
				owner = { has_valid_civic = civic_merchant_guilds }
			}
		}
		owner = {
			add_monthly_resource_mult = {
				resource = influence
				value = @tier1influencereward
				min = @tier1influencemin
				max = @tier1influencemax
			}
		}
	}
}

	}

#On first time Demetrius Cornucopia is built (Regular Empire)
planet_event = {
	id = pw_wonder.701
	title = pw_wonder.701.name
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				owner = { is_anglers_empire = no }
				AND = {
					owner = { is_anglers_empire = yes }
					NOT = { is_wet = yes }
				}
			}
		}
		text = pw_wonder.701.desc
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			owner = { is_anglers_empire = yes }
			is_wet = yes
		}
		text = pw_wonder.701.angler.desc
	}

	picture = GFX_evt_pw_demetrius_cornucopia
	show_sound = event_construction
	is_triggered_only = yes
	location = this

	trigger = {
		NOT = {owner = { has_country_flag = pw_demetrius_fields_built }}
		owner = { is_gestalt = no }
	}

	immediate = {
		owner = { set_country_flag = pw_demetrius_fields_built }
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.701.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOR = {
					has_modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_happiness
					has_modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_unity
				}
			}
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_happiness
				days = @pw_5years
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.701.b
		trigger = {
			owner = {
				has_valid_civic = civic_agrarian_idyll
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOR = {
					has_modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_happiness
					has_modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_unity
				}
			}
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_happiness
				days = @pw_10years
			}
		}
		owner = {
			add_monthly_resource_mult = {
				resource = unity
				value = @tier2unityreward
				min = @tier2unitymin
				max = @tier2unitymax
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.701.angler.desc.a
		trigger = {
			owner = {
				is_anglers_empire = yes
			}
			is_wet = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOR = {
					has_modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_happiness
					has_modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_unity
				}
			}
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_happiness
				days = @pw_10years
			}
		}
		owner = {
			add_monthly_resource_mult = {
				resource = unity
				value = @tier2unityreward
				min = @tier2unitymin
				max = @tier2unitymax
			}
		}
	}
}

	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.702.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOR = {
					has_modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_happiness
					has_modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_unity
				}
			}

				}

			}
		}
	}

#Predatory Harvesting adds Lush
planet_event = {
	id = pw_wonder.704
	title = pw_wonder.704.name
	desc = pw_wonder.704.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_pw_demetrius_cornucopia
	show_sound = event_alien_nature
	is_triggered_only = yes
	location = this

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_modifier = lush_planet }
		OR = {
			has_active_building = pw_building_demetrius_fields
			has_active_building = pw_building_demetrius_chemical_garden
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.704.a
		allow = {
			owner = {
				resource_stockpile_compare = {
					resource = food
					value >= 3000
				}
			}
		}
		add_modifier = {
			modifier = lush_planet
		}
		owner = {
			add_resource = {
				food = -3000
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.704.b
	}
}

#Land Repurposing decision Event (every resource wonder)
planet_event = {
	id = pw_wonder.790
	title = pw_wonder.790.name
	desc = pw_wonder.790.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_drilling_for_gas
	show_sound = event_alien_nature
	is_triggered_only = yes
	location = this

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_active_building = pw_building_erebus_project
			has_active_building = pw_building_erebus_fracking_plant
			has_active_building = pw_building_helios_tower
			has_active_building = pw_building_helios_translucent_obelisk
			has_active_building = pw_building_demetrius_fields
			has_active_building = pw_building_demetrius_chemical_garden
		}
		NOT = { has_planet_flag = pw_is_managing_land_purpose }
	}

	immediate = {
		set_planet_flag = pw_is_managing_land_purpose
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.790.mining
		allow = {
			owner = {
				resource_stockpile_compare = {
					resource = energy
					value >= 500
				}
			}
			NOT = { has_modifier = pw_mod_extra_mining_district }
		}
		owner = {
			add_resource = { energy = -500 }
		}
		pw_remove_land_repurposing_modifiers = yes
		add_modifier = {
			modifier = pw_mod_extra_mining_district
			clear_on_owner_change = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.790.mining_extra
		trigger = {
			owner = { has_technology = pw_tech_resource_land_repurposing_2 }
		}
		allow = {
			owner = {
				resource_stockpile_compare = {
					resource = energy
					value >= 1000
				}
			}
			NOT = { has_modifier = pw_mod_extra_mining_district_extra }
		}
		owner = {
			add_resource = { energy = -1000 }
		}
		pw_remove_land_repurposing_modifiers = yes
		add_modifier = {
			modifier = pw_mod_extra_mining_district_extra
			clear_on_owner_change = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.790.mining_max
		trigger = {
			owner = { has_technology = pw_tech_resource_land_repurposing_3 }
		}
		allow = {
			owner = {
				resource_stockpile_compare = {
					resource = energy
					value >= 2000
				}
			}
			NOT = { has_modifier = pw_mod_extra_mining_district_max }
		}
		owner = {
			add_resource = { energy = -2000 }
		}
		pw_remove_land_repurposing_modifiers = yes
		add_modifier = {
			modifier = pw_mod_extra_mining_district_max
			clear_on_owner_change = yes
		}
	}

	option = {

		allow = {
			owner = {
				resource_stockpile_compare = {
					resource = energy
					value >= 500
				}
			}
			NOT = { has_modifier = pw_mod_extra_farming_district }
		}
		owner = {
			add_resource = { energy = -500 }
		}
		pw_remove_land_repurposing_modifiers = yes
		add_modifier = {
			modifier = pw_mod_extra_farming_district
			clear_on_owner_change = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.790.farming_extra
		trigger = {
			owner = { has_technology = pw_tech_resource_land_repurposing_2 }
		}
		allow = {
			owner = {
				resource_stockpile_compare = {

			clear_on_owner_change = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.790.farming_max
		trigger = {
			owner = { has_technology = pw_tech_resource_land_repurposing_3 }
		}
		allow = {
			owner = {
				resource_stockpile_compare = {
					resource = energy
					value >= 2000
				}

			NOT = { has_modifier = pw_mod_extra_farming_district_max }

		owner = {
			add_resource = { energy = -2000 }
		}
		pw_remove_land_repurposing_modifiers = yes
		add_modifier = {
			modifier = pw_mod_extra_farming_district_max
			clear_on_owner_change = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.790.leave
		owner = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_ascension_perk = ap_mastery_of_nature }
				owner = {
					add_resource = { influence = 25 }
				}
			}
			else = {
				owner = {
					add_resource = { influence = 50 }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = { remove_planet_flag = pw_is_managing_land_purpose }
	}
}

# Astronomical Model Bureau -> id 800

#On Astronomical Model Bureau built
planet_event = {
	id = pw_wonder.800
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	pre_triggers = {
		has_owner = yes
	}

	immediate = {
		create_message = {
			type = PW_WONDER_COMPLETED
			localization = pw_message_galactic_model_complete
			days = 30
			target = this
			variable = {
				type = name
				localization = PLANET
				scope = root
			}
		}

		planet_event = { id = pw_wonder.801 }
		planet_event = { id = pw_wonder.802 }
		planet_event = { id = pw_wonder.803 days = 90 random = 30 } #Event chain begin
		owner = { country_event = { id = pw_wonder.813 days = @pw_10years }} #Event chain ends (if there is any problems along the way)
	}
}

#On first time Astronomical Model Bureau is built (Regular Empire)
planet_event = {
	id = pw_wonder.801
	title = pw_wonder.801.name
	desc = pw_wonder.801.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_pw_galactic_model
	show_sound = event_construction
	is_triggered_only = yes
	location = this

	trigger = {
		NOT = {owner = { has_country_flag = pw_galactic_model_built }}
		owner = { is_gestalt = no }
	}

	immediate = {
		owner = { set_country_flag = pw_galactic_model_built }
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.801.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOR = {
					has_modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_happiness
					has_modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_unity
				}
			}
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_happiness
				days = @pw_5years
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.801.b
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOR = {
					has_modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_happiness
					has_modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_unity
				}
			}
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_happiness
				days = @pw_5years
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			owner = { is_spiritualist = yes }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.801.c
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOR = {
					has_modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_happiness
					has_modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_unity
				}
			}
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_happiness
				days = @pw_5years
			}
		}
		owner = {
			add_monthly_resource_mult = {
				resource = unity
				value = @tier2unityreward
				min = @tier2unitymin
				max = @tier2unitymax
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			owner = { has_valid_civic = civic_byzantine_bureaucracy }
		}
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			owner = {
				#Recurring event for planet resources
				country_event = { id = pw_wonder.820 days = @pw_10years random = @pw_5years }
			}
		}
	}
}

#Tow asteroid
planet_event = {
	id = pw_wonder.803
	title = pw_wonder.803.name
	desc = pw_wonder.803.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_pw_galactic_model
	show_sound = event_cityscape
	is_triggered_only = yes
	location = this

	trigger = {
		has_active_building = pw_building_galactic_model
		NOT = { owner = { has_country_flag = pw_galactic_model_tow_asteroid }}
		NOT = { owner = { has_country_flag = pw_galactic_model_completed_corrections }}
		owner = {
			any_planet_within_border = {
				is_planet_class = pc_asteroid
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		owner = { set_country_flag = pw_galactic_model_tow_asteroid }
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.803.a
		owner = {
			random_planet_within_border = {
				limit = {
					is_planet_class = pc_asteroid
				}
				enable_special_project = {
					name = PW_TOW_ASTEROID_PROJECT
					location = this
					owner = root
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.803.b
		allow = {
			owner = { resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = influence value >= 50 }}
		}
		owner = {
			add_resource = {
				influence = -50
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				#Next event in AMB chain
				country_event = { id = pw_wonder.805 days = 180 random = 90 }
			}
		}
	}
}

#Tow asteroid (success)

			resource = unity
			value = @tier2unityreward
			min = @tier2unitymin
			max = @tier2unitymax
		}
		add_monthly_resource_mult = {
			resource = engineering_research
			value = @tier3researchreward
			min = @tier3researchmin
			max = @tier3researchmax
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			#Next event in AMB chain
			country_event = { id = pw_wonder.805 days = 90 random = 30 }
		}
	}
}

	desc = pw_wonder.805.desc

	is_triggered_only = yes
	location = this

		}
		NOT = { has_country_flag = pw_galactic_model_move_mountain }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = pw_galactic_model_completed_corrections }
		any_planet_within_border = {
			uninhabitable_regular_planet = yes
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = pw_galactic_model_move_mountain
	}

		name = pw_wonder.805.a

			}

				name = PW_MOVE_MOUNTAIN_PROJECT
				location = this
				owner = root
			}
		}
	}

		name = pw_wonder.805.b
		allow = {
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = influence value >= 100 }
		}
		add_resource = {
			influence = -100
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			#Next event in AMB chain

		}
	}
}

#Final Alignment
country_event = {
	id = pw_wonder.813
	title = pw_wonder.813.name
	desc = pw_wonder.813.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_pw_galactic_model
	show_sound = event_cityscape
	is_triggered_only = yes
	location = this

	trigger = {
		any_owned_planet = { has_active_building = pw_building_galactic_model }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = pw_galactic_model_final_alignment }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = pw_galactic_model_completed_corrections }
	}

	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = pw_galactic_model_final_alignment
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.813.a
		enable_special_project = {
			name = PW_FINAL_ALIGNMENT_PROJECT
			owner = this
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.813.b
		custom_tooltip = pw_wonder.813.b.tooltip
		add_monthly_resource_mult = {
			resource = influence
			value = @tier4influencereward
			min = @tier4influencemin
			max = @tier4influencemax
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
	}
}

#Get random planet to give resources.
country_event = {
	id = pw_wonder.820
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		is_ai = no
		any_planet_within_border = {
			NOT = { has_deposit = yes }
			OR = {
				is_asteroid = yes
				uninhabitable_regular_planet = yes
				is_planet_class = pc_gas_giant
			}
			NOT = { is_planet = event_target:pw_resource_planet }
		}
		any_owned_planet = {
			OR = {
				has_active_building = pw_building_galactic_model
				has_active_building = pw_building_aligned_galactic_model
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_planet_within_border = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_deposit = yes }
				OR = {
					is_asteroid = yes
					uninhabitable_regular_planet = yes
					is_planet_class = pc_gas_giant
				}
				NOT = { is_planet = event_target:pw_resource_planet }
			}
			save_event_target_as = pw_resource_planet
		}
		random_list = {
			40 = { #Add Minerals
				country_event = { id = pw_wonder.821 }
			}
			40 = { #Add Energy
				country_event = { id = pw_wonder.822 }
			}
			40 = { #Add Trade Value
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					can_generate_trade_value = no
				}
				country_event = { id = pw_wonder.823 }
			}
			20 = { #Add Alloys
				country_event = { id = pw_wonder.824 }
			}
			10 = { #Add Crystals
				country_event = { id = pw_wonder.825 }
			}
			10 = { #Add Gases
				country_event = { id = pw_wonder.826 }
			}
			10 = { #Add Motes
				country_event = { id = pw_wonder.827 }
			}
			1 = { #Add Dark Matter
				country_event = { id = pw_wonder.828 }
			}
			1 = { #Add Living Metal
				country_event = { id = pw_wonder.829 }
			}
			1 = { #Add Zro
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					is_materialist = yes
				}
				country_event = { id = pw_wonder.830 }
			}
		}
		country_event = {  id = pw_wonder.820 days = @pw_10years random = @pw_5years }
	}
}

#Add Minerals
country_event = {
	id = pw_wonder.821
	title = pw_wonder.821.name
	desc = pw_wonder.821.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_pw_galactic_model
	show_sound = event_cityscape
	is_triggered_only = yes
	location = event_target:pw_resource_planet

	trigger = {
		event_target:pw_resource_planet = {
			NOT = { has_deposit = yes }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.821.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:pw_resource_planet = {
					NOT = { has_deposit = yes }
				}
			}
			event_target:pw_resource_planet = {
				add_deposit = d_minerals_2
			}
		}
	}
}

# Aligned Galactic Model -> id 850

#On Aligned Galactic Model built
planet_event = {
	id = pw_wonder.850
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	pre_triggers = {
		has_owner = yes
	}

	trigger = {
		#This would be triggered every time a building is upgraded.
		last_building_changed = pw_building_aligned_galactic_model
	}

	immediate = {
		create_message = {
			type = PW_WONDER_COMPLETED
			localization = pw_message_aligned_galactic_model_complete
			days = 30
			target = this
			variable = {
				type = name
				localization = PLANET
				scope = root
			}
		}
		planet_event = { id = pw_wonder.851 }
		owner = { country_event = { id = pw_wonder.860 days = 60 }} #Spawn hidden system
	}
}

#On first time Aligned Galactic Model is built
planet_event = {
	id = pw_wonder.851
	title = pw_wonder.851.name
	desc = pw_wonder.851.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_pw_galactic_model
	show_sound = event_construction
	is_triggered_only = yes
	location = this

	trigger = {
		NOT = {owner = { has_country_flag = pw_aligned_galactic_model_built }}
	}

	immediate = {
		owner = { set_country_flag = pw_aligned_galactic_model_built }
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.851.a
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.851.b
		trigger = {
			owner = { has_valid_civic = civic_byzantine_bureaucracy }
		}
		owner = {
			add_monthly_resource_mult = {
				resource = unity
				value = @tier3unityreward
				min = @tier3unitymin
				max = @tier3unitymax
			}
		}

	}
}

#Initialize Hidden System
country_event = {
	id = pw_wonder.860
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_country_flag = pw_aligned_galactic_model_spawned_hidden_system }
		any_owned_planet = { has_active_building = pw_building_aligned_galactic_model }
	}

	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = pw_aligned_galactic_model_spawned_hidden_system

		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = pw_aligned_galactic_model_spawned_hidden_system_unique }}
			set_global_flag = pw_aligned_galactic_model_spawned_hidden_system_unique

			#Initialize Unique System
			random_owned_planet = {
				limit = { has_active_building = pw_building_aligned_galactic_model }
				solar_system = {
					spawn_system = {
						min_distance = 10
						max_distance = 30
						max_jumps = 0
						initializer = pw_capricorns_heart_system_initializer
					}
					if = {
						limit = { last_created_system = { NOT = { has_hyperlane_to = prev }}}
						add_hyperlane = {
							from = this
							to = last_created_system
						}
					}
					else = {
						add_extra_hyperlane_to_spawned_system_effect = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			#Initialize Black Hole system
			random_owned_planet = {
				limit = { has_active_building = pw_building_aligned_galactic_model }
				solar_system = {
					spawn_system = {
						min_distance = 10
						max_distance = 30
						max_jumps = 0
						initializer = special_init_01
					}
					if = {
						limit = { last_created_system = { NOT = { has_hyperlane_to = prev }}}
						add_hyperlane = {
							from = this
							to = last_created_system
						}
					}
					else = {
						add_extra_hyperlane_to_spawned_system_effect = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}

		country_event = { id = pw_wonder.861 }
	}
}
#Discover Hidden System:

	}
}

#On Tomb World in Unique System is surveyed
ship_event = {
	id = pw_wonder.862
	title = pw_wonder.862.name
	desc = pw_wonder.862.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_tomb_world
	show_sound = event_scanner
	is_triggered_only = yes
	location = from

	trigger = {
		from = {
			has_planet_flag = pw_aligned_galactic_model_tomb_world
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.862.a
		from = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_modifier = pw_mod_aligned_galactic_model_tomb_world }}
				add_modifier = {
					modifier = pw_mod_aligned_galactic_model_tomb_world
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_active_building = pw_building_polyhedron }}
				add_building = pw_building_polyhedron
			}
		}
	}
}

#After 3 years Tomb World in Unique System is colonized
planet_event = {
	id = pw_wonder.865
	title = pw_wonder.865.name
	desc = pw_wonder.865.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_asteroid_approaching_planet
	show_sound = event_air_raid_siren
	is_triggered_only = yes
	location = this

	pre_triggers = {
		has_owner = yes
		is_homeworld = no
		original_owner = yes
		is_ai = no
		is_capital = no
		is_occupied_flag = no
	}

	trigger = {
		num_pops > 0
		has_planet_flag = pw_aligned_galactic_model_tomb_world
		NOT = { has_planet_flag = pw_aligned_galactic_model_asteroid }
	}

	immediate = {
		set_planet_flag = pw_aligned_galactic_model_asteroid
		owner = {
			set_country_flag = pw_aligned_galactic_model_asteroid
		}

		create_country = {
			# name = "NAME_Incoming_Asteroid"
			name = random
			type = faction
			auto_delete = no
			flag = {
				icon = {
					category = "zoological"
					file = "flag_zoological_1.dds"
				}
				background= {
					category = "backgrounds"
					file = "new_dawn.dds"
				}
				colors={
					"black"
					"black"
					"null"
					"null"
				}
			}
			effect = {
				establish_communications_no_message = root.owner
			}
		}

		last_created_country = {
			set_country_flag = pw_incoming_asteroid

			#Spawn 5 asteroids
			create_fleet = {
				name = "NAME_pw_gerson"

						angle = random
					}

						move_to = root
						effect = {
							id = "pw_wonder.865.effect.1"
							root = {
								planet_event = { id = pw_wonder.868 }
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			create_fleet = {
				name = "NAME_pw_geras"
				effect = {
					set_aggro_range = 0
					set_fleet_stance = aggressive
					set_aggro_range_measure_from = self
					set_owner = prev
					set_fleet_flag = pw_asteroid_fleet_2
					save_event_target_as = pw_asteroid_fleet_target_2
					create_ship = {
						name = "NAME_pw_geras"
						design = "NAME_Asteroid"
					}
					set_location = {
						target = root
						distance = 60
						angle = random
					}
					queue_actions = {
						move_to = root
						effect = {
							id = "pw_wonder.865.effect.2"
							root = {
								planet_event = { id = pw_wonder.868 }
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			create_fleet = {
				name = "NAME_pw_geraldo"
				effect = {
					set_aggro_range = 0
					set_fleet_stance = aggressive
					set_aggro_range_measure_from = self
					set_owner = prev
					set_fleet_flag = pw_asteroid_fleet_3
					save_event_target_as = pw_asteroid_fleet_target_3
					create_ship = {

					}
				}

				effect = {

					set_aggro_range_measure_from = self

# On 1 Asteroid Destroyed (HIDDEN)
country_event = {
	id = pw_wonder.866
	hide_window = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		exists = from
		from = { has_country_flag = pw_incoming_asteroid }
	}

	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = pw_aligned_galactic_model_destroyed_asteroid
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = pw_aligned_galactic_model_asteroid
				from = {
					has_relation_flag = {
						who = root
						flag = pw_asteroid_enemy
					}
				}
				any_owned_planet = { has_planet_flag = pw_aligned_galactic_model_asteroid }
			}
			add_event_chain_counter = {
				event_chain = pw_multiple_asteroid_attack
				counter = pw_asteroid_destroyed
				amount = 1
			}
			random_owned_planet = {
				limit = { has_planet_flag = pw_aligned_galactic_model_asteroid }
				planet_event = { id = pw_wonder.867 }
			}
		}
		else = {
			random_country = {
				limit = {
					reverse_has_relation_flag = {
						who = from
						flag = pw_asteroid_enemy
					}
					has_country_flag = pw_aligned_galactic_model_asteroid
					any_owned_planet = { has_planet_flag = pw_aligned_galactic_model_asteroid }
				}
				add_event_chain_counter = {
					event_chain = pw_multiple_asteroid_attack
					counter = pw_asteroid_destroyed
					amount = 1
				}
				random_owned_planet = {
					limit = { has_planet_flag = pw_aligned_galactic_model_asteroid }
					planet_event = { id = pw_wonder.867 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# All Asteroid Destroyed
planet_event = {
	id = pw_wonder.867
	title = pw_wonder.867.name
	desc = pw_wonder.867.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_atmospheric_entry
	show_sound = event_ship_explosion
	location = root

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		owner = {
			has_completed_event_chain_counter = {
				event_chain = pw_multiple_asteroid_attack
				counter = pw_asteroid_destroyed
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		owner = { country_event = { id = pw_wonder.869 days = 1 }}
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.867.a
		owner = {
			add_monthly_resource_mult = {
				resource = influence
				value = @tier2influencereward
				min = @tier2influencemin
				max = @tier2influencemax
			}
			end_event_chain = pw_multiple_asteroid_attack
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.867.b
		trigger = {
			owner = { is_materialist = yes }
		}
		owner = {
			add_monthly_resource_mult = {
				resource = physics_research
				value = @tier3researchreward
				min = @tier3researchmin
				max = @tier3researchmax
			}
			add_monthly_resource_mult = {

				value = @tier3researchreward
				min = @tier3researchmin
				max = @tier3researchmax
			}
			end_event_chain = pw_multiple_asteroid_attack
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.867.c
		trigger = {
			owner = { is_militarist = yes }
		}
		owner = {
			add_monthly_resource_mult = {
				resource = influence
				value = @tier2influencereward
				min = @tier2influencemin
				max = @tier2influencemax
			}

				modifier = pw_mod_aligned_galactic_model_ready_for_asteroids
				days = @pw_5years
			}
			end_event_chain = pw_multiple_asteroid_attack
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.867.d
		trigger = {
			owner = { is_authoritarian = yes }
		}
		add_modifier = {
			modifier = pw_mod_aligned_galactic_model_suspicious_colony
			days = @pw_5years
			clear_on_owner_change = yes
		}
		owner = {
			add_monthly_resource_mult = {
				resource = influence
				value = @tier2influencereward
				min = @tier2influencemin
				max = @tier2influencemax
			}

			end_event_chain = pw_multiple_asteroid_attack
		}
	}
}

# Any Asteroid Impacts Planet
planet_event = {
	id = pw_wonder.868
	title = pw_wonder.868.name
	desc = {
		trigger = { owner = { NOT = { has_country_flag = pw_aligned_galactic_model_destroyed_asteroid }}}
		text = pw_wonder.868.desc
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { owner = { has_country_flag = pw_aligned_galactic_model_destroyed_asteroid } }
		text = pw_wonder.868.desc.some_asteroids
	}
	picture = GFX_evt_nuclear_explosion
	show_sound = event_super_explosion
	location = root
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_planet_flag = pw_aligned_galactic_model_asteroid_impacted }
	}

	immediate = {
		set_planet_flag = pw_aligned_galactic_model_asteroid_impacted
		owner = {
			country_event = { id = pw_wonder.869 days = 1 }
		}
		add_deposit = d_crater
		add_deposit = d_crater
		add_deposit = d_crater
		add_deposit = d_impact_crater
		add_deposit = d_impact_crater
		change_pc = pc_nuked
		owner = { end_event_chain = pw_multiple_asteroid_attack }
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.868.a

		if = {
			limit = { owner = { has_country_flag = pw_aligned_galactic_model_destroyed_asteroid }}
			if = {
				limit = {
					num_pops < 2
				}
				random_owned_pop = { kill_pop = yes }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					num_pops > 2
					num_pops < 6
				}
				random_owned_pop = { kill_pop = yes }
				random_owned_pop = { kill_pop = yes }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					num_pops > 6
				}
				random_owned_pop = { kill_pop = yes }
				random_owned_pop = { kill_pop = yes }
				random_owned_pop = { kill_pop = yes }
				random_owned_pop = { kill_pop = yes }
			}
			add_planet_devastation = 30
		}
		else = {
			custom_tooltip = pw_wonder.868.a.tooltip
			destroy_colony = yes
		}
	}
}

# Destroy Asteroid after fleet actions have completed and event fired
country_event = {
	id = pw_wonder.869
	hide_window = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_relation_flag = {
					who = root
					flag = pw_asteroid_enemy
				}
			}
			every_owned_ship = {
				fleet = {
					destroy_fleet = this
				}
			}
			destroy_country = yes
		}
	}
}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	}

	immediate = {

			days = 30
			target = this

				type = name
				localization = PLANET
				scope = root
			}
		}

		planet_event = { id = pw_wonder.901 }
		owner = { country_event = { id = pw_wonder.902 }}
	}
}

	id = pw_wonder.901
	title = pw_wonder.901.name
	desc = pw_wonder.901.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_announcement
	show_sound = event_construction
	is_triggered_only = yes
	location = this

	trigger = {
		NOT = {owner = { has_country_flag = pw_panopticon_built }}
	}

	immediate = {
		owner = { set_country_flag = pw_panopticon_built }
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.901.a

			limit = {
				NOR = {
					has_modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_happiness

				}
			}
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_happiness
				days = @pw_5years
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.901.b
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOR = {
					has_modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_happiness
					has_modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_unity
				}
			}
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_happiness
				days = @pw_5years
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.901.c

				value = @tier2unityreward
				min = @tier2unitymin
				max = @tier2unitymax
			}
		}

				NOR = {
					has_modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_happiness
					has_modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_unity
				}
			}
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_happiness
				days = @pw_5years
			}
		}
	}
}

#Get another empire with corrupt leader
country_event = {
	id = pw_wonder.902
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_window = yes

	trigger = {
		is_at_war = no
		is_ai = no
		any_owned_planet = {
			has_active_building = pw_building_panopticon
		}
		any_country = {
			any_neighbor_country = {
				is_ai = yes
				merg_is_default_empire = yes
				is_gestalt = no
				is_homicidal = no
				has_communications = root
				NOT = { is_at_war_with = root }
				NOT = { is_criminal_syndicate = yes }
				any_owned_leader = {
					has_trait = leader_trait_corrupt
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_neighbor_country = {
			limit = {
				is_ai = yes
				merg_is_default_empire = yes
				is_gestalt = no
				is_homicidal = no
				has_communications = root
				NOT = { is_at_war_with = root }
				NOT = { is_criminal_syndicate = yes }
				any_owned_leader = {
					has_trait = leader_trait_corrupt
				}
			}
			save_event_target_as = PWEmpireWithCorruptLeader
			random_owned_leader = {
				limit = {
					has_trait = leader_trait_corrupt
				}
				save_event_target_as = PWForeignCorruptLeader
			}
			root = { country_event = { id = pw_wonder.903 } }
		}
	}
}

#Empire with corrupt leader asks to deal with it.
country_event = {
	id = pw_wonder.903
	title = pw_wonder.903.name
	desc = pw_wonder.903.desc
	show_sound = diplomatic_notification
	is_triggered_only = yes
	location = this
	diplomatic = yes

	trigger = {
		any_owned_planet = {
			has_active_building = pw_building_panopticon
		}
	}
	picture_event_data = {
		portrait = event_target:PWEmpireWithCorruptLeader
		planet_background = event_target:PWEmpireWithCorruptLeader
		graphical_culture = event_target:PWEmpireWithCorruptLeader
		city_level = event_target:PWEmpireWithCorruptLeader
		room = event_target:PWEmpireWithCorruptLeader.ruler
	}
	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.903.a
		add_favors = {
			target = event_target:PWEmpireWithCorruptLeader
			value = 2
		}
		event_target:PWEmpireWithCorruptLeader = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				who = root
				modifier = pw_opinion_helped_with_corruption
			}
		}
		event_target:PWForeignCorruptLeader = {
			remove_trait = leader_trait_corrupt
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.903.b
		add_monthly_resource_mult = {
			resource = energy
			value = @tier3materialreward
			min = @tier3materialmin
			max = @tier3materialmax
		}
		event_target:PWEmpireWithCorruptLeader = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				who = root
				modifier = pw_opinion_helped_with_corruption
			}
		}
		event_target:PWForeignCorruptLeader = {
			kill_leader = {}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.903.c
		add_resource = {
			influence = 50
		}
		event_target:PWEmpireWithCorruptLeader = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				who = root
				modifier = pw_opinion_refused_to_help
			}
		}
	}

}

		}
	}

	immediate = {
		country_event = {
			id = pw_wonder.1003
			days = 30
			random = 30
		}
	}
}

#Get Machine Fallen empire to receive gift from
country_event = {
	id = pw_wonder.1005
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_window = yes

	trigger = {
		is_at_war = no
		is_ai = no
		any_owned_planet = {
			has_active_building = pw_building_enigma_engine
		}
		any_country = {
			merg_is_fallen_empire = yes
			is_at_war = no
			is_machine_empire = yes
			has_communications = root
			opinion = {
				who = this
				value > -70
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				merg_is_fallen_empire = yes
				is_at_war = no
				is_machine_empire = yes
				has_communications = root
				opinion = {
					who = this
					value > -70
				}
			}
			save_event_target_as = PWFallenEmpireTaskOrigin
			root = { country_event = { id = pw_wonder.1006 days = 30 random = 30} }
		}
	}
}

		add_modifier = {
			modifier = pw_mod_enigma_engine_housing
			days = -1
			clear_on_owner_change = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			planet_event = { id = pw_wonder.1012 days = 180 random = 30 }
		}
	}
}

			limit = { has_modifier = pw_mod_enigma_engine_energy }
			remove_modifier = pw_mod_enigma_engine_energy
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_modifier = pw_mod_enigma_engine_housing }
			remove_modifier = pw_mod_enigma_engine_housing
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_modifier = pw_mod_enigma_engine_art }
			remove_modifier = pw_mod_enigma_engine_art
		}
		owner = {
			add_resource = {
				influence = 50
			}
		}
	}
}

	desc = pw_wonder.1101.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_hive_mind
	show_sound = event_construction
	is_triggered_only = yes
	location = this

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.1101.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOR = {
					has_modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_happiness
					has_modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_unity
				}
			}
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_unity
				days = @pw_5years
			}
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		NOT = {owner = { has_country_flag = pw_solipsist_debate_hall_built }}
	}

	immediate = {
		owner = { set_country_flag = pw_solipsist_debate_hall_built }
	}
}

# If last tech researched was Metacognition Dialectics and minor artifacts are needed.
country_event = {
	id = pw_wonder.1102
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_ancrel = yes
		last_increased_tech = pw_tech_metacognition_dialectics
		resource_stockpile_compare = {
			resource = minor_artifacts
			value <= 10
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		country_event = {
			id = pw_wonder.1103
			days = 30
			random = 30
		}
	}
}

#Get fallen empire to receive gift from
country_event = {
	id = pw_wonder.1104
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_window = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT ={ has_country_flag = pw_sdh_fe_gift_received }
		is_at_war = no
		is_ai = no
		any_owned_planet = {
			has_active_building = pw_building_solipsist_debate_hall
		}
		any_country = {
			merg_is_fallen_empire = yes
			is_at_war = no
			OR = {
				has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_spiritualist
				has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophile
				has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_materialist
			}
			has_communications = root
			opinion = {
				who = this
				value > -70
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				merg_is_fallen_empire = yes
				is_at_war = no
				OR = {
					has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_spiritualist
					has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophile
					has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_materialist
				}
				NOT = { is_machine_empire = yes }
				has_communications = root
				opinion = {
					who = this
					value > -70
				}
			}
			save_event_target_as = PWFallenEmpireGiftOrigin
			root = { country_event = { id = pw_wonder.1105 } }
		}
	}
}

# Get gift from Fallen Empire After a Debate.
country_event = {
	id = pw_wonder.1105
	title = pw_wonder.1105.name
	desc = pw_wonder.1105.desc
	is_triggered_only = yes
	location = this
	show_sound = diplomatic_notification
	diplomatic = yes

	picture_event_data = {
		portrait = event_target:PWFallenEmpireGiftOrigin
		planet_background = event_target:PWFallenEmpireGiftOrigin
		graphical_culture = event_target:PWFallenEmpireGiftOrigin
		city_level = event_target:PWFallenEmpireGiftOrigin
		room = event_target:PWFallenEmpireGiftOrigin.ruler
	}

	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = pw_sdh_fe_gift_received
	}
	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.1105.a
		add_resource = {
			sr_dark_matter = 250
		}
		hidden_effect = { event_target:PWFallenEmpireGiftOrigin = { add_opinion_modifier = { who = root modifier = opinion_accepted_fallen_empire_request }}}
	}
	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.1105.b
		add_monthly_resource_mult = {
			resource = unity
			value = @tier3unityreward
			min = @tier3unitymin
			max = @tier3unitymax
		}
		hidden_effect = { event_target:PWFallenEmpireGiftOrigin = { add_opinion_modifier = { who = root modifier = opinion_accepted_fallen_empire_request }}}
	}
	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.1105.c
		add_resource = {
			influence = 100
		}
		hidden_effect = { event_target:PWFallenEmpireGiftOrigin = { add_opinion_modifier = { who = root modifier = opinion_refused_fallen_empire_request }}}
	}
}

# Guardian Angel -> id 1200

#On Guardian Angel built
planet_event = {
	id = pw_wonder.1200
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	pre_triggers = {
		has_owner = yes
	}

	immediate = {
		create_message = {
			type = PW_WONDER_COMPLETED
			localization = pw_message_guardian_angel_complete
			days = 30
			target = this
			variable = {
				type = name
				localization = PLANET
				scope = root
			}
		}

		planet_event = { id = pw_wonder.1201 } #Regular first time
		planet_event = { id = pw_wonder.1202 } #Gestalt first time
		planet_event = { id = pw_wonder.1203 } #Add flying fortress army

		planet_event = { id = pw_wonder.1207 days = 60 random = 30 } #Guardian Angel Peace Choice.
		planet_event = { id = pw_wonder.1204 days = @pw_halfYear } #Recursive check event

		owner = { country_event = { #Subject/Overlord events
			id = pw_wonder.1209
			days = 10
		}}
	}
}

#On first time Guardian Angel is built (Regular Empire)

	id = pw_wonder.1201
	title = pw_wonder.1201.name
	desc = pw_wonder.1201.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_landing_ship_2
	show_sound = event_construction
	is_triggered_only = yes
	location = this

		name = pw_wonder.1201.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOR = {
					has_modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_happiness
					has_modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_unity
				}
			}
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_happiness
				days = @pw_5years
			}
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		NOT = {owner = { has_country_flag = pw_guardian_angel_built }}
		owner = { is_gestalt = no }
	}

	immediate = {
		owner = { set_country_flag = pw_guardian_angel_built }
	}

#On Guardian Angel built add army
planet_event = {
	id = pw_wonder.1203
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	location = this

	trigger = {

		#While defense armies in orbit are bugged
		always = no

		OR = {
			has_active_building = pw_building_guardian_angel
			has_active_building = pw_building_stellar_sentinel
		}
		NOT = {
			any_planet_army = {
				army_type = pw_army_flying_fortress
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		create_army = {
			name = "pw_army_flying_fortress_name"
			owner = this.owner
			type = pw_army_flying_fortress
		}
	}

}

#Check if Guardian Angel was destroyed/replaced (recursive)
planet_event = {
	id = pw_wonder.1204
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	location = this

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { #Doesn't have the Guardian Angel building
				NOR = {
					has_active_building = pw_building_guardian_angel
					has_active_building = pw_building_stellar_sentinel
				}
				OR = {
					any_planet_army = { #Has the Flying Fortress
						army_type = pw_army_flying_fortress
					}
					#Has any os the deposits
					has_deposit = pw_d_guardian_angel_training
					has_deposit = pw_d_guardian_angel_police_operations
					has_deposit = pw_d_guardian_angel_tourist_attraction
					has_deposit = pw_d_guardian_angel_arena
					has_deposit = pw_d_guardian_angel_parade
					has_deposit = pw_d_guardian_angel_order_outpost
					has_deposit = pw_d_guardian_angel_scenic_set_piece
				}
			}
			planet_event = { #Remove the Fortress
				id = pw_wonder.1205
			}
			planet_event = { #Remove the Deposits
				id = pw_wonder.1208
				days = 30 #Different days, to spread the events
			}
		}
		else = {
			planet_event = { #Recursive event
				id = pw_wonder.1204
				days = @pw_halfYear
			}
		}
	}
}

# -> remove Flying Fortress
planet_event = {
	id = pw_wonder.1205
	title = pw_wonder.1205.name
	desc = pw_wonder.1205.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_landing_ship_2
	is_triggered_only = yes
	location = this

	trigger = {
		NOR = {
			has_active_building = pw_building_guardian_angel
			has_active_building = pw_building_stellar_sentinel
		}
		any_planet_army = {
			army_type = pw_army_flying_fortress
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = UNFORTUNATE
		every_planet_army = {
			limit = { army_type = pw_army_flying_fortress }
			remove_army = yes
		}
	}
}

#Guardian Angel peace choice
planet_event = {
	id = pw_wonder.1207
	title = pw_wonder.1207.name
	desc = pw_wonder.1207.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_landing_ship_2
	show_sound = event_construction
	is_triggered_only = yes
	location = this

	pre_triggers = {
		has_owner = yes
	}

	immediate = {
		remove_planet_flag = pw_guardian_angel_choice
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_deposit = pw_d_guardian_angel_training
			}
			remove_deposit = pw_d_guardian_angel_training
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_deposit = pw_d_guardian_angel_police_operations
			}
			remove_deposit = pw_d_guardian_angel_police_operations
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_deposit = pw_d_guardian_angel_tourist_attraction
			}
			remove_deposit = pw_d_guardian_angel_tourist_attraction
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_deposit = pw_d_guardian_angel_arena
			}
			remove_deposit = pw_d_guardian_angel_arena
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_deposit = pw_d_guardian_angel_parade
			}
			remove_deposit = pw_d_guardian_angel_parade
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_deposit = pw_d_guardian_angel_order_outpost
			}
			remove_deposit = pw_d_guardian_angel_order_outpost
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_deposit = pw_d_guardian_angel_scenic_set_piece
			}
			remove_deposit = pw_d_guardian_angel_scenic_set_piece
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.1207.a
		custom_tooltip = pw_wonder.1207.a.tooltip
		add_deposit = pw_d_guardian_angel_training
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.1207.b
		custom_tooltip = pw_wonder.1207.b.tooltip
		add_deposit = pw_d_guardian_angel_police_operations
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.1207.c
		custom_tooltip = pw_wonder.1207.c.tooltip
		trigger = {
			owner = { can_generate_trade_value = yes }
		}
		add_deposit = pw_d_guardian_angel_tourist_attraction
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.1207.d
		custom_tooltip = pw_wonder.1207.d.tooltip
		trigger = {
			owner = { has_valid_civic = civic_warrior_culture }
		}
		add_deposit = pw_d_guardian_angel_arena
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.1207.e
		custom_tooltip = pw_wonder.1207.e.tooltip
		trigger = {
			has_active_building = pw_building_martial_avenue
		}
		add_deposit = pw_d_guardian_angel_parade
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.1207.f
		custom_tooltip = pw_wonder.1207.f.tooltip
		trigger = {
			owner = {
				has_origin = origin_toxic_knights
				NOT = { has_country_flag = quest_abandoned }
			}
		}
		add_deposit = pw_d_guardian_angel_order_outpost
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.1207.g
		custom_tooltip = pw_wonder.1207.g.tooltip
		trigger = {
			owner = { has_valid_civic = civic_media_conglomerate }
		}
		add_deposit = pw_d_guardian_angel_scenic_set_piece
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.1207.no_peace
		custom_tooltip = pw_wonder.1207.no_peace.tooltip
	}

	after = {
		owner = {
			hidden_effect = {
				#In case the Guardian Parade is added or removed
				pw_determine_war_drive_modifier = yes
			}
		}
		set_planet_flag = pw_guardian_angel_choice
	}
}
