#On first time Feastings Grounds is built (Regular Empire)
planet_event = {
	id = pw_wonder.2701
	title = pw_wonder.2701.name
	desc = pw_wonder.2701.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_infested
	show_sound = event_construction
	is_triggered_only = yes
	location = this

	pre_triggers = {
		has_owner = yes
	}

	trigger = {
		NOT = {owner = { has_country_flag = pw_feasting_grounds_built }}
	}

	immediate = {
		owner = { set_country_flag = pw_feasting_grounds_built }
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.2701.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOR = {
					has_modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_happiness
					has_modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_unity
				}
			}
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_unity
				days = @pw_5years
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.2701.b
		trigger = {
			owner = { is_lithoid_empire = no }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOR = {
					has_modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_happiness
					has_modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_unity
				}
			}
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_unity
				days = @pw_5years
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.2701.c
		trigger = {
			owner = { is_lithoid_empire = yes }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOR = {
					has_modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_happiness
					has_modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_unity
				}
			}
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = pw_mod_wonder_built_recently_unity
				days = @pw_5years
			}
		}
	}
}

#Feasting grounds decision: choose Feast to begin
planet_event = {
	id = pw_wonder.2710
	title = pw_wonder.2710.name
	desc = pw_wonder.2710.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_infested
	show_sound = event_swarm
	is_triggered_only = yes
	location = this

	pre_triggers = {
		has_owner = yes
	}

	immediate = {
		set_planet_flag = pw_FG_is_choosing_feast
	}

	trigger = {
		has_active_building = pw_building_feasting_grounds
		NOT = { has_planet_flag = pw_FG_is_choosing_feast }
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.2710.strength_in_numbers

		allow = {
			owner = {
				#Can pay
				if = {
					limit = { is_lithoid_empire = yes }
					resource_stockpile_compare = {
						resource = minerals
						value >= 50
						mult = root.trigger:num_pops
					}
				}
				else = {
					resource_stockpile_compare = {
						resource = food
						value >= 50
						mult = root.trigger:num_pops
					}
				}
				#Does not have duplicated situation
				hidden_trigger = {
					NOT = {
						any_situation = {
							is_situation_type = pw_feasting_grounds_feast
							has_situation_flag = pw_feasting_grounds_feast_strength_in_numbers
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

		custom_tooltip = pw_wonder.2710.tooltip
		tooltip = {
			owner = {
				add_modifier = {
					modifier = pw_FG_feast_strength_in_numbers
					years = 5
				}
			}
		}

		owner = {
			#Pay the resources
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_lithoid_empire = yes
				}
				add_resource = {
					minerals = -50
					mult = root.trigger:num_pops
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_resource = {
					food = -50
					mult = root.trigger:num_pops
				}
			}
			#Start the situation
			start_situation = {
				type = pw_feasting_grounds_feast
				target = root
			}
		}
		#Adde the flag to specify which feast is it
		hidden_effect = {
			every_targeting_situation = {
				limit = {
					is_situation_type = pw_feasting_grounds_feast
				}
				set_situation_flag = pw_feasting_grounds_feast_strength_in_numbers
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.2710.driving_hunger

		allow = {
			owner = {
				#Can pay
				if = {
					limit = { is_lithoid_empire = yes }
					resource_stockpile_compare = {
						resource = minerals
						value >= 50
						mult = root.trigger:num_pops
					}
				}
				else = {
					resource_stockpile_compare = {
						resource = food
						value >= 50
						mult = root.trigger:num_pops
					}
				}
				#Does not have duplicated situation
				hidden_trigger = {
					NOT = {
						any_situation = {
							is_situation_type = pw_feasting_grounds_feast
							has_situation_flag = pw_feasting_grounds_feast_driving_hunger
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

		custom_tooltip = pw_wonder.2710.tooltip
		tooltip = {
			owner = {
				add_modifier = {
					modifier = pw_FG_feast_driving_hunger
					years = 5
				}
			}
		}

		owner = {
			#Pay the resources
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_lithoid_empire = yes
				}
				add_resource = {
					minerals = -50
					mult = root.trigger:num_pops
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_resource = {
					food = -50
					mult = root.trigger:num_pops
				}
			}
			#Start the situation
			start_situation = {
				type = pw_feasting_grounds_feast
				target = root
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_targeting_situation = {
				limit = {
					is_situation_type = pw_feasting_grounds_feast
				}
				set_situation_flag = pw_feasting_grounds_feast_driving_hunger
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.2710.sprawling_offspring
		allow = {
			owner = {
				#Can pay
				if = {
					limit = { is_lithoid_empire = yes }
					resource_stockpile_compare = {
						resource = minerals
						value >= 100
						mult = root.trigger:num_pops
					}
				}
				else = {
					resource_stockpile_compare = {
						resource = food
						value >= 100
						mult = root.trigger:num_pops
					}
				}
				#Does not have duplicated situation
				hidden_trigger = {
					NOT = {
						any_situation = {
							is_situation_type = pw_feasting_grounds_feast
							has_situation_flag = pw_feasting_grounds_feast_sprawling_offspring
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = pw_wonder.2710.tooltip
		tooltip = {
			owner = {
				add_modifier = {
					modifier = pw_FG_feast_sprawling_offspring
					years = 5
				}
			}
		}
		owner = {
			#Pay the resources
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_lithoid_empire = yes
				}
				add_resource = {
					minerals = -100
					mult = root.trigger:num_pops
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_resource = {
					food = -100
					mult = root.trigger:num_pops
				}
			}
			#Start the situation
			start_situation = {
				type = pw_feasting_grounds_feast
				target = root
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_targeting_situation = {
				limit = {
					is_situation_type = pw_feasting_grounds_feast
				}
				set_situation_flag = pw_feasting_grounds_feast_sprawling_offspring
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.2710.purpose_of_life

		allow = {
			owner = {
				#Can pay
				if = {
					limit = { is_lithoid_empire = yes }
					resource_stockpile_compare = {
						resource = minerals
						value >= 100
						mult = root.trigger:num_pops
					}
				}
				else = {
					resource_stockpile_compare = {
						resource = food
						value >= 100
						mult = root.trigger:num_pops
					}
				}
				#Does not have duplicated situation
				hidden_trigger = {
					NOT = {
						any_situation = {
							is_situation_type = pw_feasting_grounds_feast
							has_situation_flag = pw_feasting_grounds_feast_purpose_of_life
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

		custom_tooltip = pw_wonder.2710.tooltip
		tooltip = {
			owner = {
				add_modifier = {
					modifier = pw_FG_feast_purpose_of_life
					years = 5
				}
			}
		}

		owner = {
			#Pay the resources
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_lithoid_empire = yes
				}
				add_resource = {
					minerals = -100
					mult = root.trigger:num_pops
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_resource = {
					food = -100
					mult = root.trigger:num_pops
				}
			}
			#Start the situation
			start_situation = {
				type = pw_feasting_grounds_feast
				target = root
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_targeting_situation = {
				limit = {
					is_situation_type = pw_feasting_grounds_feast
				}
				set_situation_flag = pw_feasting_grounds_feast_purpose_of_life
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = pw_wonder.2710.cancel
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_planet_flag = pw_FG_is_choosing_feast
		}
	}
}
